## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="13e14-802">Windows Server 2008 屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="13e14-802">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="13e14-803">此類別包含 Windows Server 2008 的下列屬性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="13e14-803">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
